In Malayalam it is called Nellikka. In Sanskrit it is called Amlaki \" the sustainer\" in which the goddess of prosperity is inherent. Amla is the tears of Brahma , the creator god of Sanatana Dharma or Hinduism.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-S2ekRROEkFo/TmVr-8XHi0I/AAAAAAAAGA0/XkD6e6f6i2s/s1600/imagesCA9ULMD6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-S2ekRROEkFo/TmVr-8XHi0I/AAAAAAAAGA0/XkD6e6f6i2s/s1600/imagesCA9ULMD6.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nAmla has been included in the Ayurvedic texts , written in Sanskrit 7000 years ago. It is described in Charaka Samhita too.<br />\n<br />\nAmla and its flowers are used in worship, pretty much the same way as Tulsi. Amla tree is sacred in Hindusim and the tree revered as&nbsp;Mother earth.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HE8xGTWP9QU/TmVriXcaXkI/AAAAAAAAGAo/AN6aM3fq7No/s1600/imagesCA15WXHZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HE8xGTWP9QU/TmVriXcaXkI/AAAAAAAAGAo/AN6aM3fq7No/s1600/imagesCA15WXHZ.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nIt is used to make the wonder herbal tonic Chyawanprash.&nbsp; Ask any Indian abroad what Chyawanprash is, and if he does NOT know it-- kick him on his ass , kick him good-- and call him \"pseudo Indian\". <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--RcNJXEKmvI/TmVr6JNwDkI/AAAAAAAAGAw/ElwTFpEIls4/s1600/imagesCA9ABJLG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--RcNJXEKmvI/TmVr6JNwDkI/AAAAAAAAGAw/ElwTFpEIls4/s1600/imagesCA9ABJLG.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nThis 9000 year old rejuvenative Rasayana consists of 54 herbal ingredients.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CUrzvvBbJOw/TmVrpOv5mrI/AAAAAAAAGAs/QIPld8LYeG8/s1600/untitledWRT.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CUrzvvBbJOw/TmVrpOv5mrI/AAAAAAAAGAs/QIPld8LYeG8/s1600/untitledWRT.png\" /></a></div><br />\nWhen I am home on leave nowadays , I have Amla long soaked on honey as the dessert after food-- just 2 large ones. Only hot chillie taste is missing.<br />\n<br />\nThis green fruit less than an inch in diameter, has 6 vertical stripes. They should be washed with a temperature above MP, with cold interface removed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Chemicals have different thermal properties. Some will heat up very quickly, whereas others, will require substantial heating, before any temperature gain is noticed. Similarly, those cargoes that heat quickly, tend to cool down quickly, whereas the cargoes which heat slowly have far better heat retention properties. </span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The colour too matters \u2013white is a bad absorber and a bad radiator, while black is a good absorber and good radiator. These individual cargo properties should be recognised when heating cargoes on the loaded voyage. The length of the voyage must also be considered when deciding on heating schedules to avoid waste of fuel.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> above its melting point, to avoid pre-washing.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; 55 C must NOT be adjacent to cold interface<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>lest the whole bulkhead gets a solidified thick film. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Should the cargo require it, heating coils can be opened to the tank, when the liquid is at a level of approximately one metre. This can off set cumulative list at berth \u2013as for cargoes like Tallow.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If a cargo requiring heating is deemed dangerous/toxic leaks back to the engine room then \u201cDangerous/Toxic\u201d return tank is required by BCH/IBC Code.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When loading solidifying cargoes, due regard must be made to<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>ensure that lines do not become frozen.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>In any case, should stress and list/ trim conditions allow it, the tanks furthest away from the manifold should be completed first, using a sequence of working towards the shortest pipe length. In manifolds with connections both port and starboard, the opposite side to loading generally gets frozen. This must be unblocked at sea before discharge port.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 6pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Company policy requires that no tank is loaded to a volume of greater than 98% at any time. For cargoes like wine, take the permission of the chemical operator.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After loading high MP cargoes leave the pipelines open till the contents are drained properly. If proper written heating instructions are not received Master must<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Note Protest and inform the chemical operator.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If the tank is not blanketed with Nitrogen the sedimentation or build up at the tank bottom must be ascertained with sounding rod.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Charterers heating instructions must be obeyed and in any case heating increase must not exceed 5</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">C in a period of 24 hrs. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During cold weather the functioning of p/v relief valves should be checked regularly . It is possible that humid air vented from a cargo tank may condense and freeze thus inhibiting ventilation. This is also possible for cargoes with high melting point, such as Phenol, where cargo vapours could solidify in vent line<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> .<o:p></o:p></b></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For sedimented / high MP cargoes ensure that the deepwell impeller is not frozen by running the pump before arrival port with delivery valve shut.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When discharging a homogeneous heated cargo, the wing tanks should, as far as possible, be emptied before the centre tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During the discharge, several tanks may be emptied simultaneously, however when the cargo sounding becomes around 1 meter discharge of such tank must be ceased temporarily.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Final emptying, stripping and sweeping of the tanks must then happen one tank at a time.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The temperature in the tanks must be monitored and the heating must be adjusted in the tanks accordingly.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Never leave high MP cargoes inside the pipeline even for short periods like shifting barges etc.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Check out if the common collector line will get frozen.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt 6.0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When vessels are carrying solidifying products it is important that the products are at the maximum discharge temperature (or slightly above) at least one week prior to arrival at the discharge berth. Also during this period once the product is up to required temperature, soundings must be made in each tank using a rod and line to determine if there are any solid products on the tank bottom.<br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt 6.0in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt 6.0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In addition, any ballast in double bottom tanks beneath the cargo tanks MUST be lowered so that there is no direct contact between the ballast and the cargo in adjacent tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Be aware of the slope of the pump delivery deck pipes towards the manifold. Some shipyards deliberately tilt the aft of manifold pipelines to avoid fitting superstrip lines. When loading high MP cargoes in winter from barges , any delay in between two barges can freeze cargo inside pipelines . </span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If the cargo goes below the steam coils and the surveyor makes a remark that there is unpumpable then the tank must be filled up again to cover the steam coils, reheated and then discharged again. Get tank dry certificate promptly\u2014give notice to surveyor in writing in the pre-discharge CCR meeting.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After completion discharge of high MP pour point cargoes better to wash back lines using hot FW if feasible \u2013 compressed air is no use. In case of planned stop of high MP cargo in freezing weather keep the cargo recirculated. For recirculation of shore lines which can freeze discuss in the <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>preloading meeting and agree in writing. Or you may have a condition where ship is blamed for cargo frozen in unlagged or non-thermal jacketed portions of shore lines.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In order to make the tank cleaning faster and more efficient, the Master should always try to get the Dry Tank Certificate as the tanks get empty one by one \u2014especially for drying veg oils and solidifying cargoes which jam the impeller and freeze the valves.. Washing as soon as possible after receiving tank dry cert\u2014and if the terminal allows it-- will prevent some solidification and save time. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During discharge the temperature of the cargo must be at least 10 degrees C higher than the pour point of the relevant cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If vsl is discharging high MP cargoes the surveyor must be present at stripping/ sweeping time. If the discharge of high MP cargoes is stopped for any reason (shore tank change over/ barge change over/ shore leak ), the connecting hoses and lines on deck must immediately be drained back into the tank in order to avoid the system being blocked by coagulated cargo. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Any ROB noted on the certificate is clearly marked and considered by all parties as \u201cunpumpable and unreachable, non free-flowing sediments / sludge\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After dischg of vegetable oils / palm oils to prevent them from drying on the bulkheads, the bulkheads must be kept moist<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>until the tank cleaning begins. In warm weather the drying process is fast and in cold / wet weather much slower.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Hot cargo in adjacent tanks will make the residues dry very fast on the bulkheads.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Substances with a reasonable solubility (down to 0.2 %) will be removed with water. Be aware that the solubility of some chemicals increases with temperature. The wash water should be at least 15<span style=\"font-size: small;\"><sup>0</sup>C higher than the melting point of the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For Caustic potash crystallizing point is 9C while for Caustic soda it is 12 to 15C. As per the IBC code prewash for substances which have a viscosity equal to or greater than 50 mPa.s at 20\u00b0C shall be washed with hot water (temperature at least 60\u00b0C), unless the properties of such substances make the washing less effective.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">MP of a few cargoes in deg C:--<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Coconut oil/ 14-28 C<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Lard/ 33-46<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; To clean such residues it may be necessary to use a solvent like toluene.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; </span>with live steam.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"TxBrp7\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 10.2pt 85.6pt 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"TxBrp2\" style=\"line-height: normal; </span>first steaming<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the tanks <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When Graco injecting using degreasers use only one machine. Graco injection is usually 0.1% or one litre per ton of water. But for very dirty tanks 0.5% is ok. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Washing pressures and temperatures must be maintained together and must not be adjusted to compensate for either a loss in temperature by reducing the pressure and/or the number of machines. If a problem is experienced with a loss of heat, then washing may be continued, but the washing time should NOT count until the required temperature has been reached again.. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In the pre-planning stage, a proposed time scale ( bar chart ) must be formulated, to provide fore warning for the engine room. The Chief officer must also try to ensure that once pressures and temperatures have been reached, they should be kept as constant as possible, without undue fluctuations. This will avoid major fluctuations and associated problems in the engine room.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Temperature of the cleaning solution must be 20 C &gt; MP of the cargo. Temperature of the cleaning solution must be 20 C &gt; MP of the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent2\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 6pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Avoid rapid changes of temperature especially in cold weather will adversely stress the ship's structure.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent2\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 6pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When cargoes with a high wax content are carried, care must be taken that temperatures are not allowed to drop below flocculation/wax precipitation temperature as wax will not revert back into solution no matter how much the temperature is increased. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 6.0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Hence if the actual loading temperature is considerably different from the specified loading temperature the Master must protest in writing .<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>In cases of extreme temperature difference the Master may at his discretion, cease all loading operations until the matter is resolved. Keep the Chemical operator informed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "5", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6531898852329680797/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "3991708085372755531", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-09-03T22:59:00+05:30", "updated": "2014-03-07T17:12:37+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzk0MTkyNTU3NTczCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/09/queen-bee-and-darwin-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3991708085372755531", "title": "THE QUEEN BEE AND DARWIN- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oaLy3D3u3as/TmLzSj1GdCI/AAAAAAAAF_U/T6ZFGTC1ehk/s1600/qwe.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oaLy3D3u3as/TmLzSj1GdCI/AAAAAAAAF_U/T6ZFGTC1ehk/s200/qwe.png\" height=\"200\" width=\"200\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<strong><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">THE QUEEN BEE</span> </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; font-weight: normal; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></strong><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3NQtMfBc-Js/TmJi51R1G5I/AAAAAAAAF-E/elflOjYHfXM/s1600/mn.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3NQtMfBc-Js/TmJi51R1G5I/AAAAAAAAF-E/elflOjYHfXM/s320/mn.png\" height=\"156\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bees take care of the queen bee more than what they do to themselves. A hive contains thousands , but there can be only one single queen. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Her survival is important for common survival, for only the queen bee can assure the continuity of the colony. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-O01dROyhXiY/TmJi_e94U6I/AAAAAAAAF-I/JjOpEsMxh7g/s1600/imagesCABMV30I.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-O01dROyhXiY/TmJi_e94U6I/AAAAAAAAF-I/JjOpEsMxh7g/s1600/imagesCABMV30I.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen does nothing <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>but lay eggs. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>After she does the first mating, she is always inside the hive, never leaves it, and lays eggs every day from early spring through late summer. The worker bees <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>feed her and keep her clean.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There aint no difference between the egg that hatches into a queen and an egg that produces the workers. The queen is the result of selective <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>feeding with royal jelly over her six-day larval period, and emerges not as an ordinary female worker, but as one very different bee by way of <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>appearance and function. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Workers are fed royal jelly for only three days, but the queen receives it for the full six days of her larval stage and that too three times more.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All worker bees are sterile. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The queen\u2019s head and thorax are little larger than those of the workers. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The queen bee\u2019s hind legs also lack the workers\u2019 hard hairs which fringe the pollen baskets. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Though the queen hatches from exactly the same sort of egg as the workers, she lives for about five years. She is <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>longer than the male drones.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">To take life insurance , the workers raise several queens at a time, not just one. In the event that any harm befalls the old queen, a new queen immediately gets raised. So the first thing our emerging queen bee does is to find and kill the other pupating, potential queens. Leave no survivors is her motto. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the queen encounters another adult queen in the hive, the two attack each other in a fight to the finish. So when a new queen appears bursts upon the scene , <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the old queen has long since departed it, as it gets a premonition . There can be only one queen bee in the hive is essential for the establishment of discipline.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As she emerges from her cell, she first needs to mate. Mating never takes place inside the hive. The queen <span style=\"background: yellow; mso-highlight: yellow;\">leaves the hive</span> and looks for male bees\u2014drones\u2014to do JIGI JIGI and fertilize her.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-rNaVgwWX99w/TmJjYP4fh9I/AAAAAAAAF-U/cZsL6v5wGSY/s1600/imagesCAVC4S48.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-rNaVgwWX99w/TmJjYP4fh9I/AAAAAAAAF-U/cZsL6v5wGSY/s1600/imagesCAVC4S48.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are two cases which can cause the queen to leave the hive--: her mating flight and swarming time. Apart from these two occasions, the queen will never ever leave the hive. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cr5VMXvLQD8/TmJjdFD7VxI/AAAAAAAAF-Y/9fRIAMjPO5s/s1600/untitledbdw.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cr5VMXvLQD8/TmJjdFD7VxI/AAAAAAAAF-Y/9fRIAMjPO5s/s1600/untitledbdw.png\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen flies off from the hive to mate, accompanied by a group of workers. Shortly afterward, she leaves her escort of bees and flies alone to where male drones are present. When she comes within a certain distance of that area she releases a pheromone which allows the drones to locate her. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen makes from upto 10 flights during her mating period, mating with a different drone each time. Since the sperm from one male is insufficient to fill her spermatheca, she receives sperm from several males. <span class=\"dipnot\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-font-size: 12.0pt;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span>Following each fertilization, the sperm from all the males is stored together. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pDRnL7GD8iQ/TmJjkY11DII/AAAAAAAAF-c/BCyZO2iGNa4/s1600/untitledhgf.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pDRnL7GD8iQ/TmJjkY11DII/AAAAAAAAF-c/BCyZO2iGNa4/s1600/untitledhgf.png\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen will use this sperm obtained from the mating flights during her life span of 4 to 5 years. Unlike the reproductive cells in many creatures, the male bees\u2019 sperm can be preserved for years in the queen\u2019s body without losing their quantum potency. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Couple of days after <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the mating process is over, the queen starts laying eggs one by one, in a series of cells specially prepared by the worker bees. She continues the process, non-stop, each year from early spring to mid-autumn, until she kicks the bucket.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During the laying period, a queen lays from about 2800 eggs a day <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>So a single queen may lay a mid boggling 1.4 million eggs within a year. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9DVC6Jg2z3g/TmLyMUIJoEI/AAAAAAAAF_Q/uR-T423ot14/s1600/imagesCAHDZL0L.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9DVC6Jg2z3g/TmLyMUIJoEI/AAAAAAAAF_Q/uR-T423ot14/s1600/imagesCAHDZL0L.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen is able to now the gender of the other bees yet unborn. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>When the queen wishes to lay a female egg, she releases a minute amount of sperm from the spermatheca into the duct, to fertilize the egg. The egg will be fertilized only if she releases sperm. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>As a result of this process, the female bees emerge from the fertilized eggs and male bees, or drones, from the unfertilized ones.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Practically it is the worker bees who determine the gender of the egg, despite the queen\u2019s supervision of the process. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>That is because the queen lays an egg according to the kind of cell the workers have prepared for it.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jERAOFPHf-U/TmLyIBwAK-I/AAAAAAAAF_M/l_u0DeQdJnw/s1600/imagesCAY7L8S9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jERAOFPHf-U/TmLyIBwAK-I/AAAAAAAAF_M/l_u0DeQdJnw/s1600/imagesCAY7L8S9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>If the queen comes across a larger cell, then she lays an unfertilized egg in it. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This means <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the queen lays as many drone eggs as the workers have prepared male bee cells for., not any more-- not any less<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The workers also determine the number of cells. On the basis of the needs of the hive, they decide how many worker and how many drone cells should be constructed, and how much space should be reserved for honey or pollen .<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bees have very small brains, but has amazingly good <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>judgment about the need of future social order.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4HGfwib8UVU/TmLyDvJzSZI/AAAAAAAAF_I/jDUSwYupdNA/s1600/imagesCAH8BUZS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4HGfwib8UVU/TmLyDvJzSZI/AAAAAAAAF_I/jDUSwYupdNA/s1600/imagesCAH8BUZS.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They lick up the chemical from the queen\u2019s body and transmit it to the other bees during food transfer, which takes place by mouth. During this process, the odor released by the queen is quickly transmitted to all other members of the colony. This means that all of the colony\u2019s members share a common odor, distinguishing them from members of other colonies. There is no need to wear uniform.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The odor of this queenly substance prevents the workers from raising a new queen, so such indications are a signal for the worker bees. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>As its level reduces, the workers immediately begin to construct new royal cells and set about raising new queens. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yg2O621f-GA/TmLx_rWbzSI/AAAAAAAAF_E/JyE1afpi1Ss/s1600/imagesCADOQY7M.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yg2O621f-GA/TmLx_rWbzSI/AAAAAAAAF_E/JyE1afpi1Ss/s1600/imagesCADOQY7M.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the colony finds itself facing the danger of having no queen, the worker bees immediately start feeding some of the existing larvae with royal jelly. The workers start to tear down the walls of cells to widen the regular cells and enlarge them into royal cells. Several worker cells are torn down for any single royal cell. The worker larvae inside them die in this process.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They prefer the survival of a few candidate queens to that of several workers.. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Shortly afterwards, the first of the specially reared queens emerges from her cell and sets about eliminating her rivals. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bees possess a unique consciousness.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lkNFcy8O6Ts/TmLx6QStbcI/AAAAAAAAF_A/uy9UJSjvQfE/s1600/imagesCAAT5MDD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lkNFcy8O6Ts/TmLx6QStbcI/AAAAAAAAF_A/uy9UJSjvQfE/s1600/imagesCAAT5MDD.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The males, or drones make no contribution to the defense of the hive, nor to cleaning, nor to food gathering. Their only function is to do JIGI JIGI with the queen&nbsp; to fertilize her, and die.. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are very distinctive differences between male and female bees. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only females have stings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only female bees construct combs.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only females do the ass shakin\u2019 waggle dance .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only females are able to collect nectar.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only females <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>nurse the young.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-nWEqioX-ZB4/TmJjrsOGOcI/AAAAAAAAF-g/QWCHWiFpwwc/s1600/imagesCA3E2E28.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-nWEqioX-ZB4/TmJjrsOGOcI/AAAAAAAAF-g/QWCHWiFpwwc/s1600/imagesCA3E2E28.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In winter, only female bees are to be found in the hive, because the males drones are either kicked out from the hive or if they act too stubborn, they are killed , much before winter\u2019s arrival. As spring approaches, however, the worker bees begin to build cells for male eggs. The queen then lays in these cells eggs which will hatch into drones. The males emerge from these cells in early May.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EWI-CVNb01s/TmLx2Y0kU7I/AAAAAAAAF-8/nUrkowOSQQQ/s1600/imagesCA91VQBB.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EWI-CVNb01s/TmLx2Y0kU7I/AAAAAAAAF-8/nUrkowOSQQQ/s1600/imagesCA91VQBB.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Despite the male bees\u2019 lack of abilities, the female workers take great care of them until they do JIGI JIGI <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>with the queen. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Half a dozen <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>workers need to work non-stop to spoon feed just one of the 400 to 500 male bees in the hive. In other words, some 2,000 to 3,000 worker bees do nothing else than care for the drones for a specific period of time.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">No more than 10 males are necessary for the queen to mate. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Yet, a bee community raises hundreds of drones. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2s3P5LBMuqo/TmJjx6dIghI/AAAAAAAAF-k/2uH-DfxYZrc/s1600/imagesCAY65WPQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2s3P5LBMuqo/TmJjx6dIghI/AAAAAAAAF-k/2uH-DfxYZrc/s1600/imagesCAY65WPQ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The male bees leave the hive and start looking for the queen some two weeks after they emerge from their cells. The males can locate the queen during her mating flight, as she lets out a scent. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VjYnZjMHm2Y/TmLxy2r4IvI/AAAAAAAAF-4/lkqq_T5_KuY/s1600/imagesCA04VQZY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VjYnZjMHm2Y/TmLxy2r4IvI/AAAAAAAAF-4/lkqq_T5_KuY/s1600/imagesCA04VQZY.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The males need to be able to fly at a height for long periods while searching for the queen and to be able to locate her scent from a long distance away. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The queen and the male generally meet at high altitudes. The males are unable to approach the queen at lower than 15 feet . During mating, part of the males\u2019 reproductive organs, including the sperm sac, rupture, and as soon as mating is completed, the male bee dies. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Neither do the other males who fail to mate with the queen have much longer to live. Males live only in spring and early summer, after which they are killed by the workers. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iZ9rx92pfSg/TmLxuDNFXzI/AAAAAAAAF-0/ZxTMCJeW8jo/s1600/imagesCA7WH1IX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iZ9rx92pfSg/TmLxuDNFXzI/AAAAAAAAF-0/ZxTMCJeW8jo/s1600/imagesCA7WH1IX.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Once the time of the mating flight is over\u2014and as the nectar levels in flowers start to decline in the heat of summer\u2014the female workers\u2019 loving , coy behavior towards the males changes completely. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Although the workers look after the males very carefully during the mating period, once the JIGI JIGI <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>job is done , they start to tear off the drones\u2019 wings and attack them. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the males try to eat anything, the workers seize them in their powerful mouths and drag them by their antennae or legs to the hive entrance and throw them out. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Expelled in this disgraceful manner, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the males soon die of hunger, since they lack the ability to find nectar.. Therefore, as a last resort, they make determined efforts to re-enter the hive. Yet again they face the bites and poisoned stings of the workers. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Although the drones are larger than the workers, they sort of acquiesce to this female attack. <span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">They dont fight back.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">F</span>ollowing the expulsion of all the males from the hive, the females\u2014both workers and the queen\u2014spend a long peaceful <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>time in the hive, until spring the following year, on their own.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div align=\"left\" class=\"ANAMETIN\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 8.5pt 0pt 0in; text-align: left; text-indent: 28.35pt;\">\n</div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\">Suck on this post Darwin\u2014</span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">You said survival of the fittest and ability to withstand change and all that, right?&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oW0MA-QAOjI/TmLs7zawDyI/AAAAAAAAF-w/2M1TMluJNmU/s1600/imagesCA6ZURW9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
