, &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Bhagavad Gita, Chapter IV, Verse 7.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Hey Bhaarata (Arjuna). It is Faith which teaches renunciation and is responsible for the elevation and well-being of human beings. Whenever in the passage of time, <span class=\"s2\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">(yadaa yadaa)</span></span> Faith (or dharma) is weakened or is under attack, <span class=\"s2\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">(glaanirbhavati)</span></span> - and whenever adharma spreads without control <span class=\"s2\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">(abhyutthaanam.h)</span></span> - it is then <span class=\"s2\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">(tadaatmaanM)</span></span> that I re-incarnate myself <span class=\"s2\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">(sRRijaamyaham.h) </span></span>with all my powers to restore Faith.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4Q8iw83n_jI/TmH5bMRfKDI/AAAAAAAAF9Y/idLGzkc4Vs4/s1600/imagesCAH7OOOL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4Q8iw83n_jI/TmH5bMRfKDI/AAAAAAAAF9Y/idLGzkc4Vs4/s1600/imagesCAH7OOOL.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">It is the function of God as Vishnu, the protector of the world, to keep the world going on the lines of righteousness. He assumes birth to re-establish right when wrong prevails.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/szuOU-g4h-g/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/szuOU-g4h-g&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/szuOU-g4h-g&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">I am quoting this Sanskrit verse from memory, as this world\u2019s oldest language which was used for writing the Vedas in 5000 BC, was compulsory in my school Kendriya Vidyalaya till 9<sup>th</sup> standard. It was very easy for me , because high literature Malayalam ( my mother tongue in Kerala ) is very close to Sanskrit.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Kerala is very important when you talk of Indian history, as India was protected by the Himalayas in the north, and very few souls knew the treacherous passes of Bholan and Khyber through the frozen Hindu Kush range. You take a chance and you die a painful death.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Alexander the great had a marital alliance with a dark skinned Indian girl by the name of Roxanna, 2300 year ago, to secure the secrets of this pass. Almost all dealings with foreign people was via Kerala ships. Mecca, Petra and Jerusalem was on the spice caravan routes. All 3 sites had Shiva Temples with powerful Shiva lingam black meterorite stones. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Palestine was Palistan, Kaaba was Kabalishwara.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">In 7000 BC when Indian Aryan Emperor ruled from Jesusalem to Urals to Vietnam\u2014there was only one religion in the world, the Sanatana Dharma or Hinduism. In 1900 BC, a Indian by the name of Gautama Buddha was the first to make a new religion in an opportunistic manner, so that people would pray to him , rather than to God. The excuse he gave was that the common man needs to understand the spiritual teachings in his own vernacular lingo. He was indeed successful as at one time half the world were Buddhists.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Buddhism, Christianity and Islam are offshoots of Hinduism. Jesus Christ was in Calicut Kerala for 3 years to learn meditation , dowsing and healing , before he burst upon the scene at Jerusalem, as per readings of Edgar Cayce. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Before reaching Jerusalem he visited the Egyptian pyramids, and he had a dark skinned and long haired woman Mary Magdalene with him on the ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Now <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>let me get back to the subject--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Trillions of words has been written about the Lost civilization of Atlantis by Western historians over brandy and cigars. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>All funding by poor tax payer\u2019s money.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>A lot of them have given ridiculous <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>twists , including exact latitude and longitude of&nbsp; the sunken&nbsp;Atlantis ( sic! ) -- to the diabolically doctored versions of Akashic chronicles reader Edgar Cayce. The correct trance readings of Edgar Cayce have been sunk by the Vatican, as the Pope did not want a Catholic to speak about Hindu religion icons.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Now let me recount a written account of Shiva Purana , which is 7000 years old, about ATALA or Atlantis.. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">There was an demon <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>named Tara whose son was Taraka. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Taraka went to a Madhuvana forest and started a very severe penance or tapasya. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He stood on one toe of one leg , gazing at the sun with arms raised. He drank only water .<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Then after several years he stood upside down on his hands, without drinking water, deriving energy by gazing at the sun..Then he hung upside down on the branches of a very tall tree. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Lord Brahma could no longer ignore the great energy emanating from him and he asked Taraka to ask for a boon. Taraka said \u201c If you are pleased with me , please grant me two boons . The first boon is that no one created by you should be as strong as me. The second boon is that I can be killed only by Shiva\u2019s son\u201d. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Shiva at that point in time had no sons. Sati had died and although she had been reborn as Parvati, she had not yet married Shiva. Brahma in haste , granted Tarakasura the two boons. </span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">The demon went to a city named Shonitapura and put up camp there. All the other demons made Tarakasura who was already famous, their king. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Thanks to the boon, Tarakasura was so strong that the easily defeated all his challengers, and started harassing all at will, being low in moral fibre. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Tarakasura pretty soon had three asura sons named Vidyunmali, Tarakaksha and Viryavana (Tripura-asuras). <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>These three also started a similar severe penance as done by their father . </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Brahma had no choice but to appear before them, and told tem to ask for a boon.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Taraka asura\u2019s sons immediately said \u201c Make us immortal\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Brahma relpied \u201c There is no way <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I can make you immortal, for it is beyond my power . Instead ask for something else\u201d <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">OK then , said Viyunamali, Tarakaksha and Viryavana \u2013 this was their scheme even before they started their penance . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"postbody\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Grant us the following boons \u201c <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Let three floating forts be made. The first will be of gold, the second of silver and the third of iron. We will live in these forts . If anyone can destroy Tripura ( three floating forts ) with one single arrow, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>only then can death be destined for us\u201d. </span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Again Brahma granted the boon in great haste. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Brahma asked the Danava architect <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>named Maya to <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>build the three forts, in a great mandala . The golden fort was built in heaven, the silver one in the sky and the iron one on earth. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Tarakaksha got the golden fort, Viryavana the silver one and Vidyunmali the iron one. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Each of the forts was a huge self contained <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>city , with glittering palaces and space ships inside, in a 3D mandala of 3 bubbles\u2014powered by crystals and solar energy. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">The gods soon became concerned with the wanton and debauched life inside Tripura. The maharishis were getting disturbed and they had complained. The gods first went to Brahma ( creator god ) who refused to listen to their tales. The gods then went to Shiva ( destroyer god ) for help, but Shiva took the Brahma line. The gods then went to Vishnu ( preserver god ), who suggested that the problem was that the demons were doing nothing wrong officially, the solution could be to persuade them to become sinners, which will get Shiva upset. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Using his divine powers Vishnu contacted a man. This man\u2019s head was sclean haven, his clothes were faded and he carried a wooden water-pot in his hands. He covered his mouth with a piece of cloth . \"What are my orders?\" he asked Vishnu. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Vishnu replied \u201c <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I will teach you a religion that is completely against the Vedas. You will then get the impression that there is no Svarga (heaven) and no Naraka (hell) and that both heaven and hell are on earth. You will not believe that rewards and punishments for deeds committed on earth are meted out after death. Go to Tripura and teach the demons this religion, by which they are dislodged from the righteous path. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Only then we can do something about Tripura \u201d . </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">This man and four of his disciples went to a forest that at Tripura and began to preach. They were so convincing that soon they converted citizens by the hundreds. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Even sage Narada got confused and was converted. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Narada who loved to gossip, carried news of this wonderful new religion to king Vidyunmati.. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Since a great sage Narada had converted. Vidyunmati also accepted the new religion. And in due course, so did the other two brothers Tarakaksha and Viryavana. The demons gave up revering the Vedas and they broke the black Shiva lingam stones. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"postbody\">Vishnu immediately rushed to Shiva , knowing he had to make him angry&nbsp;said \u201c Tripura should be destroyed. , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Western historians and the Pope blurred&nbsp;&nbsp;Jesus and Orpheus , and pretty soon it was Jesus who was attributed to all the qualities of Orpheus \u2013 enchanting wild animals with a 7 stringed lyre .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The original sitar ( derived from the veena&nbsp;&nbsp;) has seven strings&nbsp;&nbsp;which run over curved, raised frets ( Rudra / Saraswati veena) , and the remainder are sympathetic strings (tarb,&nbsp;&nbsp;taarif , tarafdaar) which run underneath the frets and resonate in sympathy with the played strings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">It was Orpheus who gave Pythagoras&nbsp;&nbsp;the mathematical relations of the notes on the musical scale.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The wisdom of the ancients has been taught by the philosophers of Greece, but also by people called Jews in Syria, and by Brahmins in India.\"--Megasthenes- 300 BC.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">This is about the efforts of Orpheus to retrieve his wife, Eurydice, (who was killed by a serpent on their wedding night ) from the underworld. Orpheus went down to Hades to claim her, and played so sweetly with his lute that Pluto allowed Eurydice to return to the earth with Orpheus, but on condition that he did not look behind him until he had reached the terrestrial regions. Orpheus, however, in his anxiety to see if she were following him, looked round, and Eurydice disappeared from his sight, instantly and forever.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">This LOOKING BACK story is mirrored from the lore of Adi Shankaracharya bringing Devi to Kerala in 2000 BC \u2014&nbsp;&nbsp;he looked back and Devi disappeared at the spot of Mookambika temple at Kollur Karnataka.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Pythagoras learnt metempsychosis from India.&nbsp;&nbsp;Metempsychosis is the Greek equivalent of the 11000 year old Vedic Hindu doctrine of transmigration of the soul, Karma and and reincarnation after death.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Almost every Greek text tells that Orpheos was famous for Ahimsa or non-violence . In Euripides' play Hippolytos a father taunts his son with the \"lifeless food\" he eats since taking Orpheos for his \"king.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Orpheus is praised for his knowledge of medicine and astrology ( ONLY Ayurveda and Indian astrology existed those days).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Punch into Google search-<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>MIHIRA MUNI , THE GREAT ASTROLOGER CUM ASTRONOMER VADAKAYIL</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The name of India, so far as is known, first appears in Greek literature in the 5th century B.C. in the works of Hekataios and Herodotos.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Herodotos of Halikarnassos (484-425 B. C.) whose histories have survived in their entirety had written clearly about India .&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Herodotos writes about India's population, saying that the Indians are \"more in number than any nation known to me.\u201d&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">He goes to great details while telling of Kerala\u2019s&nbsp;&nbsp;wealth in gold; He tells about&nbsp;&nbsp;Indian birds and beasts he regards as much bigger than those existing elsewhere, except for horses. Once when Socrates was asked by an Indian seer, what he does for a living . When Socrates replied that he \"investigated human life,\" the Indian laughed aloud , saying that \"no one was able to observe human affairs if he was ignorant of divine matters and consciousness .\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Vegetarianism in Greece is called Orphikos bios, or \"Orphic way of life\". Hinduism is a recent term coined by the invaders.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M2xgVDTSgN0/Tl9bPlZ06pI/AAAAAAAAF3k/mcu4SEVO8tk/s1600/ss.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M2xgVDTSgN0/Tl9bPlZ06pI/AAAAAAAAF3k/mcu4SEVO8tk/s1600/ss.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">SANATANA</span> </span></strong>means <strong><span style=\"font-size: large;\">\" <span style=\"color: red;\">that which holds eternal Vedic knowledge</span>\"--</span></strong> encompassing&nbsp;everything from microcosm to macrocosm. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XcvytzEdLjM/Tl9YhE8_I7I/AAAAAAAAF2o/6Kjcn4hNOr0/s1600/nsw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XcvytzEdLjM/Tl9YhE8_I7I/AAAAAAAAF2o/6Kjcn4hNOr0/s1600/nsw.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><strong>DHARMA</strong></span> means \"<strong><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"> righteousness</span></strong>\".&nbsp; Dharma leads to eternal bliss,&nbsp;both in this world and the next. It is your sole and soul companion after death.&nbsp; Human acts without conscience which creates&nbsp;conflict is called Adharma. This is the reason why India has never invaded any other country. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C5UYtczw5Bs/Tl9awQ3fRHI/AAAAAAAAF3Y/U1gLj2rZkGE/s1600/images%252B%2525282%252529%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C5UYtczw5Bs/Tl9awQ3fRHI/AAAAAAAAF3Y/U1gLj2rZkGE/s1600/images%252B%2525282%252529%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Dharma leads you on the path of self realisation. Dharma includes adhara or regulation of daily life as per your conscience and written Vedic laws. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The fundamentals of Dharma as per the Bhagwat Gita are-- respect, truth, grace,&nbsp;restraint, love, non-violence, restraint, lack of jealousy and greed, knowledge of self and austerity.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Rs-4Fjd2F3g/Tl9SlMrhZkI/AAAAAAAAF2U/Vba-z2oJ-KY/s1600/imagesCASAG2MV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Rs-4Fjd2F3g/Tl9SlMrhZkI/AAAAAAAAF2U/Vba-z2oJ-KY/s1600/imagesCASAG2MV.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is the mother of all religions.&nbsp; It is 11500 years old, while the next oldest religion is just 2500 years old.&nbsp; Its spiritual books the Vedas were written in Sanskrit 7000 years ago&nbsp;, when the rest of the world was doing grunt grunt for communications.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fwcz7leRs8o/Tl9a-ByjKiI/AAAAAAAAF3c/IZwTDUA3C-Y/s1600/images%252B%25252870%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fwcz7leRs8o/Tl9a-ByjKiI/AAAAAAAAF3c/IZwTDUA3C-Y/s1600/images%252B%25252870%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Sanatana Dharma respects the planet along with its flora and fauna. It is the only religion which advocates vegetarianism. Manu , the ancient law giver was a committed environmentalist. Manu wrote that polluting the environment was a punishable offence.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hUcRWGgT1NM/Tl9ZYFBLT3I/AAAAAAAAF2s/Owjcg1G5o_4/s1600/images%252B%2525281%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hUcRWGgT1NM/Tl9ZYFBLT3I/AAAAAAAAF2s/Owjcg1G5o_4/s1600/images%252B%2525281%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Manu\u2019s laws in Manava Dharma Shastra , are in 100000 verses in 24 books and was propagated from Jerusalem to Urals to Vietnam in 7000 BC by the great Indian Emperor who ruled these lands. These laws were given 5300 years before Hammurabi who lifted wholesale from these laws, leaving aside kindness to the environment and social grace. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qz0erZnrOdE/Tl9Zi3Y9zzI/AAAAAAAAF2w/x9cjLQGmXHc/s1600/cjp.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qz0erZnrOdE/Tl9Zi3Y9zzI/AAAAAAAAF2w/x9cjLQGmXHc/s1600/cjp.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In Manu\u2019s laws a person could be ex-communicated from society for mindless felling of tress or killing of animals, the way the English speaking white man shot the buffalo and exterminated the Indian American , or how the Australian Aborigine race was exterminated.. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MRChOGfq5t0/Tl9bxzla61I/AAAAAAAAF30/bJM1YI7zfGs/s1600/images%252B%25252836%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MRChOGfq5t0/Tl9bxzla61I/AAAAAAAAF30/bJM1YI7zfGs/s1600/images%252B%25252836%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In Manu\u2019s laws destruction of nature was the destruction of the state. Yet we Indians get lectured by the West daily, nowadays , on antipollution and the need to be environment friendly. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-n0Z--2hH2ro/Tl9bIJZ7T1I/AAAAAAAAF3g/kX_Yg4iNIh4/s1600/mfw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-n0Z--2hH2ro/Tl9bIJZ7T1I/AAAAAAAAF3g/kX_Yg4iNIh4/s1600/mfw.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The whole idea of Vaastu was to construct something without disturbing the flow of nature and interrupting natural flow of energy. It is about peaceful co-existence and comfort.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hindu Vedas and mantras revere, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>nay , worship nature , and its flora and fauna. Many animals and birds were vehicles of god. The deities of Hinduism permeate the world of nature.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Earth is personified as Godess Bhudevi , the consort of Lord Vishnu- the preserver, the middle prong of Shiva\u2019s<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Tamas Rajas (yin-yang)<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>trishul . <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">Mata Bumih Putroaham prithviahah. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Earth is my mother and I am her son.<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">You don\u2019t have to live in India to be a Hindu. You could be a Catholic living in England, as long as you have a conscience, live in harmony with nature ,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>grateful for her natural bounties, do not dominate and harass other living beings, have inherent grace and know your \u201cduties\u201d.. You must understand that human beings are just but a link in this symbiotic chain of life and consciousness.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bQiIOXxRRUI/Tl9bY91KOkI/AAAAAAAAF3o/2j1ZwJ8mK10/s1600/imagesCAHKSGLU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bQiIOXxRRUI/Tl9bY91KOkI/AAAAAAAAF3o/2j1ZwJ8mK10/s1600/imagesCAHKSGLU.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There can be NO inquisition in Hinduism. When the heroic Catholic Templar knights embraced Hinduism after excavating Solomon\u2019s temple , they were burnt at the stake by the Vatican. If these knights wanted they could have run all over France and the Vatican. It was their new vegetarian \u201cPagan\u201d faith which prevented them from doing so.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;By the way Jesus Christ became a vegetarian ( so was Mary Magdalene&nbsp;) after he visited Kerala for learning meditation and healing.</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">You cannot be a Hindu heretic , because there is no standard set of dogmas in Hindu faith , written or unwritten, from which deviation could make you a heretic.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Openness is the essence of Hinduism. </span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fDT3rzGWEZc/Tl9bdj2dliI/AAAAAAAAF3s/LPE_BOqOswA/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fDT3rzGWEZc/Tl9bdj2dliI/AAAAAAAAF3s/LPE_BOqOswA/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Gratitude is inherent, which makes this religion noble . Example: A Hindu will never ever neglect his aged and vulnerable parents</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Divorce rate within Hindus is the lowest in the world--it is a mindset . Marriage is NOT based on lust, but by sacred commitment of 7 pheras around a holy fire. No Hindu woman will go for silicon implants to save her marriage.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">A true Hindu will not exploit vulnerability. Hinduism does not allow you to breach a trust. When a Hindu says \"thank you\", he really means it. When a Hindu greets you with a Namaste, he bows to the greatness in you.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There is great tolerance to other cultures and spiritual paths. The heart of Hinduism is oneness and inclusivity..&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Vedic rishis had stressed, there are many paths to the final goal.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2g66Rz2WQ9I/Tl9bq8yin1I/AAAAAAAAF3w/893ES9Iq9kc/s1600/images%252B%2525288%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2g66Rz2WQ9I/Tl9bq8yin1I/AAAAAAAAF3w/893ES9Iq9kc/s1600/images%252B%2525288%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is why Hinduism has a multiplicity of Gods and Goddesses. This is why Hinduism abjures all divides and separates. It happily embraces all different paths.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">15% of the people on this planet are Hindu. It evolved in 9000 BC. In 7000 BC Hindu temples existed from Jerusalem to Urals to Vietnam-- during the benevolent rule of Aryan Indian king Emperor Vikramaditya.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is a spiritual code. Know thyself is the quintessence.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It has no founder or a Supreme head. There is NO supreme middleman like the Pope who can canonise a human into a saint, by&nbsp;hoodwinking the unsuspecting masses.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a movement based on principles or evolved over time code of Dharma. It is a relentless pursuit of truth, flexible to suit all situations.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hinduism does NOT care for individual leadership or hierarchy.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is the wonder of Hinduism. I don't care to visit temples, I don't care to pray, yet--I am a believing and practising Hindu.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is the world's oldest religion 11000 years old, when the white man's land was under the quaternary ice age sheets.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Yet, <span style=\"color: blue;\">Hinduism is NOT a religion. It is a way of life</span>.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">This is a religion without fundamentals or lack of compulsions.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> You cannot get ex-communicated for NOT toeing the line.</span></span><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is why India has never attacked any other country in the past history, but has been invaded again and again and again</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;. It is NOT that we did NOT know how to fight--our 6000 year old 3 metre long Kerala Urumi swords broke the sound barrier.</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/sbWuk5AjHhg/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n\n\n\n\n\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a faith so unique, that it gives space for every other religion. Hinduism has never claimed to be the only true religion.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hinduism has never converted , by guile ( Christian missionaries ) or force ( Muslim ) -- nor has a army of missionaries , ramming it down unwilling throats.</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I feel happy as a Hindu to meet people of other faiths, and converse with them, without being burdened by the conviction , that my religion is the best, and I have embarked on the right path, that every one else has missed.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Though we use the Bhagawat Gita to swear an oath, as set down by our British rulers in court-- we do NOT have a single holy book, like the Bible or Koran. Such has been the tolerance to deviant beliefs.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sh5Nen8lLgQ/Tl9cbYVjQRI/AAAAAAAAF4I/JycEqOzBumA/s1600/imagesCAUBA2PG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sh5Nen8lLgQ/Tl9cbYVjQRI/AAAAAAAAF4I/JycEqOzBumA/s1600/imagesCAUBA2PG.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I am proud of the diversity, the range, and the lofty metaphysical aspirations of Vedanta. </span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The eternal truths in the Vedas were written by our great seers without junk DNA in their bodies and king sized resonating pineal glands. It is NOT mere speculation of guesswork.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At the heart of Hinduism remains mans' essential quest for union with the Absolute supreme.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-snfOwM4Axt8/Tl9cWMpH3-I/AAAAAAAAF4E/AXA7ZYKYtcw/s1600/mgw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-snfOwM4Axt8/Tl9cWMpH3-I/AAAAAAAAF4E/AXA7ZYKYtcw/s1600/mgw.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is based on reason and NOT faith--unless the faith is an extension of reason. It has its own beliefs, timeless traditions, ethics, rituals, philosophy and theology.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Vedas evolved in 7000 BC, but was penned down in 5000 BC, on the banks of the Saraswati. It is NOT a set of preconceived ideas.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The fundamental deities are Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva. ( Creator/ preserver/ destroyer ) or Tamas/ Sattva Rajas of the Yin Yang trident.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ancient India has survived over 12000 years, because Hinduism was developed along Spiritual lines, NOT materialistic lines.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism is a living organism-- a vast tree with countless branches.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For Sanatana Dharma , time is cyclic-like seasons. It is NOT linear like the concept of other religions, which made them focus on death rather than life and NOW..&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Most Hindus believe in the doctrine of reincarnation. This is the belief that each of us has a soul and that our souls are involved in a cycle of birth, death and rebirth.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Reincarnation is tied closely to the doctrine of karma. <span style=\"color: blue;\">Karma is the belief that the actions during the previous life determine the conditions of each person's birth.&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">This is the only religion that <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>has NOT reduced itself to one man, one book, one faith.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hindus themselves prefer to use the Sanskrit term </span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">sanatana dharma</span><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> </span><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">for their religious tradition. <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">Sanatana </span>as \u201ceternal moral order\u201d encourages Hindus to seeks and moral truth wherever it might be found, each individual must realize this truth through his or her own systematic effort. </span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hindu scripture, based on the insights of Hindu sages and seers, serves primarily as a guidebook. But ultimately truth comes to us through direct consciousness of the divine or the ultimate reality. as GOD. Hindus refer to it as Brahman.. (This is not to be confused with Brahmin meaning priest.) </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In many religions truth is delivered or revealed from a divine source and enters the world through a single agent: for example, Abraham in Judaism, Jesus Christ in Christianity, and Muhammad in Islam. These truths are then recorded in scriptures that serve as a source of knowledge of divine wisdom: the Hebrew Bible, the New Testament of the Christian Bible, and the Koran. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In the Hindu tradition, by contrast, there is no single revelation, &nbsp;by which people may achieve knowledge of the divine or lead a life backed by religious law. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Hindu tradition acknowledges that there are many paths by which people may seek and experience religious understanding and direction. It also claims that every individual has the potential to achieve enlightenment. .&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hinduism\u2019s universal world-view and its willingness to accept and celebrate diverse philosophies, deities, symbols, and practices, makes it a religion that emphasizes similarities and shared characteristics rather than differences. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Hindu tradition , unlike other religions --has always concerned itself with the human situation rather than the Hindu situation. Instead of basing its identity on separating Hindu from non-Hindu or believer from non-believer, Hinduism has sought to recognize principles and practices that would lead any individual to become a better human being and understand and live in harmony with dharma. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The distinction of dharma from the Western sense of religion is crucial to understanding Hindu religious identity Dharma is an all-important concept for Hindus. In addition to tradition and moral order, it also signifies the path of knowledge and correct action.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Because of Hinduism\u2019s emphasis on living in accordance with dharma, anyone who is striving for spiritual knowledge and seeking the right course of ethical action is, in the broadest sense, a follower of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">sanatana dharma</span>.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\">The chain of births and deaths\u2014is called samsara.</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\">Samsara</span><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\"> is caused by a lack of knowledge of our true self and our resultant desire for fulfilment outside ourselves. We continue to embody ourselves, or be reborn, in this infinite and eternal universe as a result of these unfulfilled desires. </span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\">The chain of births lets us resume the pursuit. The law that governs <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">samsara</span> is called karma. Each birth and death we undergo is determined by the balance sheet of our <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>\u2014that is, in accordance with the actions performed and the dispositions acquired in the past.</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\">Karma</span><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\"> is a crucial Hindu concept. According to the doctrine of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>, our present condition in life is the consequence of the actions of our previous lives. The choices we have made in the past directly affect our condition in this life, and the choices we make today and thereafter will have consequences for our future lives in <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">samsara</span>.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-o55fFHVxye4/Tl9b410CEVI/AAAAAAAAF34/1pmVzvwM7KE/s1600/679380823_dca7e21647.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-o55fFHVxye4/Tl9b410CEVI/AAAAAAAAF34/1pmVzvwM7KE/s1600/679380823_dca7e21647.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>This is why I can go for a function in Calicut and walk back home at midnight with my wife loaded with gold jewellery. The poor homeless sleeping on the street without food in their stomachs and no possessions other than a loincloth would not dream of attacking my wife.</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; line-height: 115%;\">An understanding of this interconnection, according to Hindu teachings, can lead an individual towards right choices, deeds, thoughts, and desires, without the need for an external set of commandments. Under the doctrine of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">karma</span>, the ability to make choices remains with the individual.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-2EovvrPXwG8/Tl9b_CZkWFI/AAAAAAAAF38/PXAnB5qfAH4/s1600/download%252B%2525282%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-2EovvrPXwG8/Tl9b_CZkWFI/AAAAAAAAF38/PXAnB5qfAH4/s1600/download%252B%2525282%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;\">The sacred fire serves as a witness to the vows exchanged between the bride and the bridegroom. Fire is the only thing on this planet which cannot be polluted. The sacrament of death calls for cremation (burning of the dead body), at the end of which the ashes are collected and deposited, usually by the sea side&nbsp;or in a river.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;\">Hindu gods are regularly displayed with their female counterparts. Tantra involves the balancing of these two aspects\u2014Shiva (representing consciousness) and Shakti (representing energy)\u2014in a manner reminiscent of yin and yang.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5cGvlPTw0xQ/Tl9cGAFh51I/AAAAAAAAF4A/pIOs3Q3AUUw/s1600/imagesCAFF8I5C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5cGvlPTw0xQ/Tl9cGAFh51I/AAAAAAAAF4A/pIOs3Q3AUUw/s1600/imagesCAFF8I5C.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18pt; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hinduism has neither a beginning or founder, nor a central authority, hierarchy, or organization.<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\"> </span>a. A further characteristic of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Hinduism</span> is the ideal of ahimsa. Ahimsa, \u201cnon-injury\u201d or the absence of the desire to harm, is regarded by Indian thinkers as one of the keystones of their ethics. Historically, ahimsa is unrelated to vegetarianism</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wsRzacwelsk/Tl9TFECc-TI/AAAAAAAAF2k/Qxe2iBV1ccM/s1600/imagesCAV7SSQS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp; <span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">  </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">TOLERANCE: <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>The Templar knights got converted to Hinduism ( PAGAN religion ) after laying their hands on the concealed Hindu literature in Malayalam and Sanskrit, from the underground vaults <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>of King Solomon\u2019s temple. They went into the Ahimsa mode ( non-violent ) . There is NO other explanation that hundreds of these ruthless marauding and seasoned knights allowed themselves to be tortured and burnt at the stake.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">  </span><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Jews have never been persecuted in Kerala over the millenniums. Orpheus, however, in his anxiety to see if she were following him, looked round, and Eurydice disappeared from his sight, instantly and forever.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">This LOOKING BACK story is mirrored from the lore of Adi Shankaracharya bringing Devi to Kerala in 2000 BC \u2014&nbsp;&nbsp;he looked back and Devi disappeared at the spot of Mookambika temple at Kollur Karnataka.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Pythagoras learnt metempsychosis from India.&nbsp;&nbsp;Metempsychosis is the Greek equivalent of the 11000 year old Vedic Hindu doctrine of transmigration of the soul, Karma and and reincarnation after death.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Almost every Greek text tells that Orpheos was famous for Ahimsa or non-violence .
